Marathon Petroleum Corp. (NYSE&#58; MPC) today reported net income attributable to MPC of $4.5 billion, or $9.06 per diluted share, for the third quarter of 2022, compared with net income attributable to MPC of $694 million, or $1.09 per diluted share, for the third quarter of 2021. </font></div><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;margin-top:9pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Adjusted net income was $3.9 billion, or $7.81 per diluted share, for the third quarter of 2022. This compares to adjusted net income of $464 million, or $0.73 per diluted share, for the third quarter of 2021. Adjusted results for third-quarter 2022 exclude net pre-tax benefits of approximately $1 billion and for third-quarter 2021 exclude pre-tax charges of $48 million. Adjustments are shown in the accompanying release tables.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;margin-top:9pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Adjusted earnings before interest, taxes, depreciation, and amortization (adjusted EBITDA) was $6.8 billion for the third quarter of 2022, compared with $2.4 billion for the third quarter of 2021. </font></div><div id="id29ec07e2d974433be84e5f65326f727_4"></div><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;margin-top:9pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#8220;Market demand for our products remains strong, and our third-quarter results reflect our improving operational and commercial execution,&#8221; said President and Chief Executive Officer Michael J. Hennigan.  &#8220;We completed our $15 billion share repurchase commitment and announced an increase to our quarterly dividend of approximately 30%.&#8221; </font></div><div id="id29ec07e2d974433be84e5f65326f727_13"></div><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;margin-top:9pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%">Refining &#38; Marketing (R&#38;M)</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;margin-top:9pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Segment adjusted EBITDA was $5.5 billion in the third quarter of 2022, versus $1.2 billion for the third quarter of 2021. Segment adjusted EBITDA excludes refining planned turnaround costs, which totaled $384 million in the third quarter of 2022 and $205 million in the third quarter of 2021. The increase in segment adjusted EBITDA was driven by higher margins and volumes.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;margin-top:9pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">R&#38;M margin was $30.21 per barrel for the third quarter of 2022, versus $14.51 per barrel for the third quarter of 2021. Crude capacity utilization was approximately 98%, resulting in total throughput of 3.0 million barrels per day for the third quarter of 2022. This compares to crude capacity utilization of approximately 93% for the third quarter of 2021, which resulted in total throughput of 2.8 million barrels per day. </font></div><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;margin-top:9pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Refining operating costs per barrel were $5.63 for the third quarter of 2022, versus $4.97 for the third quarter of 2021. The majority of this increase was driven by higher energy costs, as well as $0.13 per </font></div><div style="height:72pt;position:relative;width:100%"><div style="bottom:0;position:absolute;width:100%"><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;margin-top:6pt"><font><br></font></div><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;margin-top:9pt;text-align:right"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">2</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;margin-top:9pt;text-align:right"><font><br></font></div></div></div><hr style="page-break-after:always"><div style="min-height:72pt;width:100%"><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;margin-top:9pt"><font><br></font></div></div><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;margin-top:9pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">barrel of non-recurring costs recorded in the quarter associated with a multi-year property tax assessment.  </font></div><div id="id29ec07e2d974433be84e5f65326f727_16"></div><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;margin-top:9pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%">Midstream</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;margin-top:9pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Segment adjusted EBITDA was $1.5 billion in the third quarter of 2022, versus $1.4 billion for the third quarter of 2021, up roughly 9% year over year.   </font></div><div id="id29ec07e2d974433be84e5f65326f727_19"></div><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;margin-top:9pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%">Corporate and Items Not Allocated</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;margin-top:6pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Corporate expenses totaled $173 million in the third quarter of 2022, compared with $186 million in the third quarter of 2021.</font><font style="color:#ee2724;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%"> </font></div><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;margin-top:6pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">In the third quarter of 2022, items not allocated to segments include a $549 million non-cash gain for the contribution of the Martinez assets to the Martinez Renewables joint venture and a $509 million non-cash gain related to an MPLX LP (NYSE&#58;MPLX) third-party contract reclassification</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:5.85pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;position:relative;top:-3.15pt;vertical-align:baseline">(a)</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">. These have been excluded from the company&#8217;s adjusted results.</font></div><div id="id29ec07e2d974433be84e5f65326f727_22"></div><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;margin-top:9pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%">Speedway </font></div><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;margin-top:9pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">This business was sold on May 14, 2021. Historic results are reported as discontinued operations. </font></div><div id="id29ec07e2d974433be84e5f65326f727_25"></div><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;margin-top:9pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%">Financial Position, Liquidity, and Return of Capital </font></div><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;margin-top:9pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">As of September 30, 2022, MPC had $11.1 billion of cash, cash equivalents, and short-term investments and $5 billion available on its bank revolving credit facility. MPC debt at the end of the third quarter of 2022 totaled $6.9 billion, excluding MPLX debt. MPC&#8217;s gross debt-to-capital ratio, excluding MPLX debt, was 21% at the end of the third quarter of 2022. </font></div><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;margin-top:9pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">In October, MPC completed its $15 billion return of capital commitment, having repurchased approximately 30% of outstanding shares as of the program commencement. The company has approximately $5 billion remaining available under its current share repurchase authorizations.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;margin-top:9pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Today, MPC announced that the Board of Directors approved an increase to the quarterly dividend to $0.75 per share. The dividend is payable December 12, 2022 to shareholders of record on November 16, 2022.   </font></div><div id="id29ec07e2d974433be84e5f65326f727_28"></div><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;margin-top:9pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%">Strategic and Operations Update</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;margin-top:9pt"><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">The Martinez Renewables joint venture with Neste closed on September 21, 2022. All required closing conditions were met, including the receipt of the necessary permits and regulatory approvals. The first phase of the Martinez renewables project facility is expected to be mechanically complete by year-end 2022. Initial production capacity is expected to be 260 million gallons per year of renewable fuels. Pretreatment capabilities are expected to come online in the second half of 2023 and the facility is expected to be capable of producing 730 million gallons per year by the end of 2023.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;margin-top:9pt"><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">The Midstream segment remains focused on executing the strategic priorities of strict capital discipline, embedding a low-cost culture, and optimizing the portfolio. MPLX continues to evaluate opportunities to meet the needs of today and participate in an energy-diverse future. </font></div><div style="height:72pt;position:relative;width:100%"><div style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:700;line-height:120%">Non-GAAP Financial Measures </font></div><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;margin-top:9pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Management uses certain financial measures to evaluate our operating performance that are calculated and presented on the basis of methodologies other than in accordance with GAAP. We believe these non-GAAP financial measures are useful to investors and analysts to assess our ongoing financial performance because, when reconciled to their most comparable GAAP financial measures, they provide improved comparability between periods through the exclusion of certain items that we believe are not indicative of our core operating performance and that may obscure our underlying business results and trends. These measures should not be considered a substitute for, or superior to, measures of financial performance prepared in accordance with GAAP, and our calculations thereof may not be comparable to similarly titled measures reported by other companies. The non-GAAP financial measures we use are as follows&#58;</font></div><div id="id29ec07e2d974433be84e5f65326f727_82"></div><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;margin-top:9pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:700;line-height:120%">Adjusted Net Income Attributable to MPC</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;margin-top:9pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Adjusted net income attributable to MPC is defined as net income attributable to MPC excluding the items in the table below, along with their related income tax effect. We have excluded these items because we believe that they are not indicative of our core operating performance and that their exclusion results in an important measure of our ongoing financial performance to better assess our underlying business results and trends. </font></div><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;margin-top:9pt;padding-right:6.75pt"><font calculated by applying a combined federal and state tax rate of 22% to the pre-tax adjustments. The corresponding adjustments to reported income taxes are shown in the table above. </font></div><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;margin-top:3pt;padding-left:18pt;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:5.85pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;position:relative;top:-3.15pt;vertical-align:baseline">(b)</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;padding-left:10.87pt">Weighted average diluted shares used for the adjusted net loss per share calculations do not assume the conversion of share-based awards, as the effect would be anti-dilutive.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:3pt;margin-top:3pt;text-indent:18pt"><font><br></font></div><div id="id29ec07e2d974433be84e5f65326f727_85"></div><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;margin-top:9pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:700;line-height:120%">Adjusted EBITDA </font></div><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;margin-top:9pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Amounts included in net income (loss) attributable to MPC and excluded from adjusted EBITDA include (i) net interest and other financial costs&#59; (ii) provision&#47;benefit for income taxes&#59; (iii) noncontrolling interests&#59; (iv) depreciation and amortization&#59; (v) refining planned turnaround costs and (vi) other adjustments as deemed necessary, as shown in the table below. We believe excluding turnaround costs from this metric is useful for comparability to other companies as certain of our competitors defer these costs and amortize them between turnarounds. </font></div><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;margin-top:9pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Adjusted EBITDA should not be considered as a substitute for, or superior to income (loss) from operations, net income attributable to MPC, income before income taxes, cash flows from operating activities or any other measure of financial performance presented in accordance with GAAP. e.removeAttribute('id');a.parentNode.appendChild(e)}}
if(e)e.style.display='block';Show.LastAR=e};Show.hideAR=function(){Show.LastAR.style.display='none'};Show.toggleNext=function(a){var e=a;while(e.nodeName!='DIV')e=e.nextSibling;if(!e.style){}else if(!e.style.display){}else{var d,p_;if(e.style.display=='none'){d='block';p='-'}else{d='none';p='+'}
